2026-02-28T14:10:57.9350501Z     14. # Address PR Reviews
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9350728Z     15. 
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9351992Z     16. This skill automates the process of addressing feedback on an open Pull Request. It prioritizes code integrity by analyzing surrounding symbols to resolve reviewer typos (SOLID Principles + Levenshtein Distance) and handles problematic feedback by drafting clarifying questions.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9353191Z     17. 
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9353364Z     18. ## Usage
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9353629Z     19. 1. Ensure you are in a git repository with an open PR.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9353989Z     20. 2. Run the skill to fetch unresolved threads.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9354411Z     21. 3. For each thread, analyze the feedback and determine if it is actionable.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9354888Z     22. 4. Apply approved fixes locally or draft empathetic replies.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9355326Z     23. 5. Run a verification command to validate changes.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9355612Z     24. 
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9355794Z     25. ## Analysis Criteria
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9356008Z     26. 
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9356269Z     27. For each review thread, you (the invoking LLM) must determine:
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9356596Z     28. 
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9356802Z     29. ### Actionable Feedback
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9357147Z     30. - The suggestion improves code quality, correctness, or clarity.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9358235Z     31. - The fix adheres to SOLID principles (e.g., single responsibility, open/closed, dependency inversion) and maintains the function's expected behavior and type contracts.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9359684Z     32. - If the reviewer has a typo (e.g., "identifer" instead of "identifier"), use **Levenshtein Distance** to fuzzy-match against actual code symbols and infer the correct intent.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9360435Z     33. - The change is within the scope of this PR.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9360716Z     34. 
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9360893Z     35. **Output:**
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9361086Z     36. ```json
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9361266Z     37. {
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9361448Z     38.   "isActionable": true,
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9361750Z     39.   "patch": "corrected code snippet or full replacement",
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9362166Z     40.   "explanation": "why this fix is correct and maintains contracts"
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9362514Z     41. }
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9362684Z     42. ```
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9362851Z     43. 
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9363033Z     44. ### Problematic Feedback
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9363471Z     45. - The suggestion is out of scope (e.g., "re-architect the whole auth flow" on a helper function PR).
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9363964Z     46. - The feedback is vague or uninformed.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9364318Z     47. - The reviewer may have misunderstood the code or PR intent.
2026-02-28T14:10:57.9364644Z     48.

2026-02-28T14:11:01.0740254Z   name: view
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0740641Z   args:
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0741145Z     path: /home/runner/work/ai/ai/src/skills/pr-review-handle/SKILL.md
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0742077Z     view_range: |
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0742387Z       [
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0742654Z         55,

2026-02-28T14:11:01.0743407Z       ]
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0750705Z   result: |
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0751155Z     55. ```
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0751660Z     56. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0752141Z     57. ## Script
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0752857Z     58. The execution logic is located in `scripts/address-reviews.js`.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0753683Z     59. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0754051Z     60. ## Workflow for the Invoking LLM
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0754642Z     61. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0754922Z     62. 1. Extract each review thread (file, line, comment body).
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0755639Z     63. 2. Read the local file context (±15 lines around the commented line).
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0756136Z     64. 3. Extract symbols from the code context and tokens from the reviewer comment.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0756902Z     65. 4. Compute **Levenshtein Distance** between comment tokens and code symbols to detect reviewer typos (threshold: 3, adaptive to token length).
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0757562Z     66. 5. Analyze the feedback:
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0758320Z     67.    - Review the fuzzy match suggestions (e.g., "identifer" → "identifier", distance: 1).
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0758862Z     68.    - Is it fixing a typo? Verify the intended symbol exists in context.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0759424Z     69.    - Does it adhere to SOLID principles and maintain the code's expected behavior and type contracts?
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0759905Z     70.  - Is it actionable and in scope?
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0760212Z     71. 6. Provide your analysis as a JSON response.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0760587Z     72. 7. The skill will apply patches and prompt for verification.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0760911Z     73. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0761139Z     74. ### Fetching online review threads from CLI/API
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0761966Z     75. - Use GitHub CLI directly: `gh pr view <pr-number> --json reviewThreads,reviews,comments` (uses your existing GitHub auth; no third-party tooling).
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0763236Z     76. - REST fallback via the CLI: `gh api repos/:owner/:repo/pulls/:number/reviews` plus `gh api repos/:owner/:repo/pulls/:number/comments` (add `--paginate` if needed). Both return the same online review content shown in the PR UI.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0764105Z     77. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0764291Z     78. ## Levenshtein Distance
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0764517Z     79. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0765377Z     80. The skill uses [Levenshtein Distance](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Levenshtein_distance) (edit distance) to fuzzy-match symbols mentioned in reviewer comments against actual identifiers in the surrounding code. This compensates for:
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0766302Z     81. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0766640Z     82. - **Reviewer typos**: "identifer" → "identifier" (distance 1)
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0767157Z     83. - **Misspelled variable names**: "getUserNme" → "getUserName" (distance 1)
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0767672Z     84. - **Transposed characters**: "recieve" → "receive" (distance 2)
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0768405Z     85. - **Missing/extra characters**: "usr" near "user" (distance 1)
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0768742Z     86. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0768921Z     87. ### How it works
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0769122Z     88. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0769897Z     89. 1. **Symbol extraction**: All identifiers (variable names, function names, properties) are extracted from the ±15 lines of code context. Common JS keywords are filtered out.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0771178Z     90. 2. **Comment tokenization**: Potential symbol references are extracted from the reviewer's comment — both backtick-quoted code spans and bare camelCase/snake_case tokens.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0772602Z     91. 3. **Fuzzy matching**: Each comment token is compared against every code symbol. If the Levenshtein distance is > 0 and ≤ the adaptive threshold (min of 3 or half the shorter string's length), it's flagged as a likely typo.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0773809Z     92. 4. **Output**: Matches are presented to the invoking LLM with the original token, the best matching symbol, and the edit distance to inform the analysis.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0774646Z     93. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0774957Z     94. ## Example
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0775149Z     95. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0775419Z     96. **Thread**: "Change `usr.id` to `user.identifer`"
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0775818Z     97. **Context**: File shows `const user = { id: 123, identifier: "abc" }`
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0776161Z     98. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0776342Z     99. **Levenshtein Matches**:
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0776640Z     100. - `usr` → `user` (distance: 1)
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0776973Z     101. - `identifer` → `identifier` (distance: 1)
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0777252Z     102. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0777433Z     103. **Your Analysis**:
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0778083Z     104. - Typo detected: "identifer" → "identifier" (confirmed by Levenshtein distance of 1)
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0778610Z     105. - "usr" likely refers to "user" (distance: 1)
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0778922Z     106. - Both symbols exist in scope.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0779280Z     107. - Check function signature: does it expect `id` or `identifier`?
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0779770Z     108. - If `identifier` matches the contract, it's actionable.
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0780079Z     109. 
2026-02-28T14:11:01.0780255Z     110. **Response**:
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7289394Z 
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7290185Z function:
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7290843Z   name: edit
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7292204Z   args:
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7294478Z     new_str: |
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7294854Z       ## Script
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7295396Z       The execution logic is located in `scripts/address-reviews.js`.
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7296003Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7296309Z       ### Implementation Details
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7296692Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7297320Z       The script uses `gh api` extensively for direct REST API access, providing:
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7298395Z       - **Granular control**: Fetch specific data from different endpoints
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7299321Z       - **Pagination support**: Automatically handle large result sets with `--paginate`
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7300256Z       - **Better metadata**: Access review state, timestamps, diff hunks, and more
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7301072Z       - **Efficient fetching**: Query only the data needed for analysis
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7301566Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7301749Z       #### API Endpoints Used
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7301968Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7302265Z       1. **Pull Request Reviews** (`gh api repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pr}/reviews`)
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7303136Z          - Fetches review-level data including state (APPROVED, CHANGES_REQUESTED, COMMENTED)
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7303662Z          - Provides reviewer information and overall review metadata
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7304049Z          - Supports pagination for PRs with many reviews
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7304328Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7304607Z       2. **Review Comments** (`gh api repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pr}/comments`)
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7305110Z          - Fetches line-specific code comments with file paths and line numbers
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7305497Z          - Includes diff hunks for context
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7305884Z          - Provides threading information (in_reply_to_id) for conversation tracking
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7306315Z          - Supports pagination for large review threads
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7306587Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7306819Z       3. **PR Information** (`gh pr view --json number,url`)
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7307187Z          - Gets basic PR metadata to identify which PR to analyze
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7307483Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7307662Z       #### Advantages over `gh pr view`
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7308102Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7308355Z       - Direct REST API access provides richer data structures
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7308751Z       - Pagination ensures all comments are fetched (no truncation)
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7309124Z       - More control over filtering and data processing
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7309773Z       - Better support for resolving ambiguities with additional context fields
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7310340Z       - Can be extended to post comments/reviews back to GitHub
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7310646Z     old_str: |

2026-02-28T14:11:16.7335435Z       ### Fetching Review Threads with gh api
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7335902Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7336359Z       The skill leverages `gh api` for direct GitHub REST API access:
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7337098Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7337769Z       **Primary Method (Recommended):**
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7338747Z       ```bash
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7340834Z       # Fetch all reviews with pagination
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7341504Z       gh api repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pr_number}/reviews --paginate
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7342091Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7342526Z       # Fetch all review comments (line-specific) with pagination
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7343232Z       gh api repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pr_number}/comments --paginate
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7343789Z       ```
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7344060Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7344348Z       **Why gh api?**
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7344910Z       - **Pagination**: Use `--paginate` to automatically fetch all pages of results
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7345859Z       - **Rich Metadata**: Access fields like `diff_hunk`, `position`, `in_reply_to_id`, review state
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7346773Z       - **No Third-Party Tools**: Uses your existing GitHub authentication
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7347594Z       - **REST API Standard**: Direct access to documented GitHub API endpoints
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7348686Z       - **Scriptable**: Easy to parse JSON responses and filter data programmatically
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7349326Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7349627Z       **Alternative (Legacy):**
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7350016Z       ```bash
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7350343Z       # Simpler but less flexible
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7350891Z       gh pr view <pr-number> --json reviewThreads,reviews,comments
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7351444Z       ```
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7351713Z       
2026-02-28T14:11:16.7352010Z       **GraphQL Option (Advanced):**

2026-02-28T14:11:30.3055087Z     +
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3055564Z     +The script uses `gh api` extensively for direct REST API access, providing:
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3056385Z     +- **Granular control**: Fetch specific data from different endpoints
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3057279Z     +- **Pagination support**: Automatically handle large result sets with `--paginate`
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3058377Z     +- **Better metadata**: Access review state, timestamps, diff hunks, and more
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3059209Z     +- **Efficient fetching**: Query only the data needed for analysis
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3059912Z     +
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3060226Z     +#### API Endpoints Used
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3060616Z     +
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3061144Z     +1. **Pull Request Reviews** (`gh api repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pr}/reviews`)
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3062205Z     +   - Fetches review-level data including state (APPROVED, CHANGES_REQUESTED, COMMENTED)
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3063138Z     +   - Provides reviewer information and overall review metadata
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3063754Z     +   - Supports pagination for PRs with many reviews
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3064391Z     +
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3064736Z     +2. **Review Comments** (`gh api repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pr}/comments`)
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3065342Z     +   - Fetches line-specific code comments with file paths and line numbers
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3065739Z     +   - Includes diff hunks for context
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3066129Z     +   - Provides threading information (in_reply_to_id) for conversation tracking
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3066858Z     +   - Supports pagination for large review threads
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3067395Z     +
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3067672Z     +3. **PR Information** (`gh pr view --json number,url`)
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3068443Z     +   - Gets basic PR metadata to identify which PR to analyze
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3068775Z     +
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3068957Z     +#### Advantages over `gh pr view`
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3069193Z     +
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3069423Z     +- Direct REST API access provides richer data structures
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3069815Z     +- Pagination ensures all comments are fetched (no truncation)
2026-02-28T14:11:30.3070187Z     +- More control over filtering and data processing

2026-02-28T14:12:18.0975106Z     +
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0975615Z     +The script uses `gh api` extensively for direct REST API access, providing:
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0976460Z     +- **Granular control**: Fetch specific data from different endpoints
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0977320Z     +- **Pagination support**: Automatically handle large result sets with `--paginate`
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0978413Z     +- **Better metadata**: Access review state, timestamps, diff hunks, and more
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0979226Z     +- **Efficient fetching**: Query only the data needed for analysis
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0979781Z     +
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0980069Z     +#### API Endpoints Used
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0980453Z     +
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0980970Z     +1. **Pull Request Reviews** (`gh api repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pr}/reviews`)
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0981943Z     +   - Fetches review-level data including state (APPROVED, CHANGES_REQUESTED, COMMENTED)
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0982836Z     +   - Provides reviewer information and overall review metadata
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0983511Z     +   - Supports pagination for PRs with many reviews
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0984003Z     +
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0984480Z     +2. **Review Comments** (`gh api repos/{owner}/{repo}/pulls/{pr}/comments`)
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0985334Z     +   - Fetches line-specific code comments with file paths and line numbers
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0986043Z     +   - Includes diff hunks for context
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0986733Z     +   - Provides threading information (in_reply_to_id) for conversation tracking
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0987517Z     +   - Supports pagination for large review threads
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0988311Z     +
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0988722Z     +3. **PR Information** (`gh pr view --json number,url`)
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0989391Z     +   - Gets basic PR metadata to identify which PR to analyze
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0989929Z     +
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0990262Z     +#### Advantages over `gh pr view`
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0990682Z     +
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0991090Z     +- Direct REST API access provides richer data structures
2026-02-28T14:12:18.0991793Z     +- Pagination ensures all comments are fetched (no truncation)
